+void AppSendRangingDataPX4(phRangingData_t *pRangingData)
+{
+	static distance_msg_t DATA; //set 0 ?
+	const uint16_t len = 0x0020;
+
+	if (pRangingData == NULL) {
+		return;
+	}
+
+	DATA.cmd = 0x83;
+	DATA.len = len;
+	DATA.seq_ctr = pRangingData->seq_ctr;
+
+	memcpy(&DATA.sessionId, &pRangingData->sessionId, sizeof(DATA.sessionId));
+	DATA.range_interval = pRangingData->curr_range_interval;
+
+	memcpy(&DATA.MAC, pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].mac_addr, sizeof(DATA.MAC));
+	memcpy(DATA.measurements.MAC, pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].mac_addr, sizeof(DATA.MAC));
+
+	DATA.measurements.status 					= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].status;
+	DATA.measurements.nLos 						= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].nLos;
+	DATA.measurements.distance 					= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].distance;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_azimuth 				= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_azimuth;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_elevation 			= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_elevation;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_dest_azimuth 			= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_dest_azimuth;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_dest_elevation 		= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_dest_elevation;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_azimuth_FOM 			= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_azimuth_FOM;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_elevation_FOM 		= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_elevation_FOM;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_dest_azimuth_FOM 		= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_dest_azimuth_FOM;
+	DATA.measurements.aoa_dest_elevation_FOM 	= pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_dest_elevation_FOM;
+
+	DATA.stop = 0x1B; 		// Should be 0x1B
+
+	/* Send Data */
+	APPSENDDATA(&DATA, sizeof(DATA));
+
+
+
+    /* Display data on DEBUG*/
+	if((pRangingData->seq_ctr % 64 )== 0){
+		/* this debug output is considerably slowing down code and therefore ranging execution:
+		 * But if desired can be turned on to receive live data viewable from the console*/
+		const double deg2rad = M_PI / 180.0;
+		double distance = (double)(pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].distance);
+		double azimuth = (double)(pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_azimuth) / 128;
+		double elevation = (double)(pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_elevation) / 128;
+		double dest_azimuth = (double)(pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_dest_azimuth) / 128;
+		double dest_elevation = (double)(pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].aoa_dest_elevation) / 128;
+
+		/* ****** Position algorithm ************************************
+		* this algorithm takes distance and angle measurements (spherical coordinates) and converts them into the cartesian bodyframe expected by the LTE
+		* Convert spherical coordinates to cartesian: sph(r, phi, theta) => cartesian(x,y,z)
+		* With radial distance r, elevation angle theta, azimuth angle phi
+		*
+		* position =   ( r * cos(elevation) * cos(azimuth),
+		* 		( r * cos(elevation) * sin(azimuth),
+		* 		( r * sin(elevation) )
+		*
+		* The resulting coordinate system is not NED (north-east-down)
+		* Using the angle information from the drone device results in a position where the Drone is centered at [0, 0, 0] in NED.
+		* ||Using the angle information from the destination device results in a position where the ground device is centered at [0, 0, 0] in NED.||
+		* The coordinates "rel_pos_*" are the position of the landing point relative to the vehicle.
+		* To change POV we negate rotate the position with Eulerangles[XYZ] = [-90 0 -90]:
+		*
+		* rotation_matrix = (0, 1, 0,
+				0, 0, 1;
+				-1, 0, 0);
+		*
+		* This step can also be skipped if we rearrange the position calculation like this:
+		* 	X -> -Z
+		* 	Y -> X
+		* 	Z -> Y
+		* Resulting in the following conversion function:
+		* ******************************************/
+		double z = distance * cos(azimuth * deg2rad) * cos(elevation * deg2rad);
+		double y = distance * sin(azimuth * deg2rad) * cos(elevation * deg2rad);
+		double x = -distance * sin(elevation * deg2rad);
+
+		PRINTF("%d; %d; %d; %.1f; %.1f; %.1f; %.1f; %.1f; %.1f; %.1f\r\n",
+				pRangingData->seq_ctr,
+				pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].nLos,
+				pRangingData->ranging_meas.range_meas_twr[0].distance,
+				azimuth,
+				elevation,
+				dest_azimuth,
+				dest_elevation,
+				x, y, z);
+	}
+}
 #endif // UWBIOT_APP_BUILD__DEMO_CDC

+typedef struct UWB_range_meas{
+	uint8_t MAC[2];					// MAC address of UWB device
+	uint8_t status;					// Status of Measurement
+	uint16_t distance; 				// Distance in cm
+	uint8_t nLos; 					// line of sight y/n
+	int16_t aoa_azimuth;			// AOA of incoming msg for Azimuth antenna pairing
+	int16_t aoa_elevation;			// AOA of incoming msg for Altitude antenna pairing
+	int16_t aoa_dest_azimuth;		// AOA destination Azimuth
+	int16_t aoa_dest_elevation; 	// AOA destination elevation
+	uint8_t aoa_azimuth_FOM;		// AOA Azimuth FOM
+	uint8_t aoa_elevation_FOM;		// AOA Elevation FOM
+	uint8_t aoa_dest_azimuth_FOM;	// AOA Azimuth FOM
+	uint8_t aoa_dest_elevation_FOM;	// AOA Elevation FOM
+} __attribute__((packed)) UWB_range_meas_t;
+
+
+typedef struct distance_msg{
+	uint8_t cmd;      			// Should be 0x8E for distance result message
+	uint16_t len; 				// Should be 0x30 for distance result message
+	uint32_t seq_ctr;			// Number of Ranges since last Start of Ranging
+	uint32_t sessionId;			// Session ID of UWB session
+	uint32_t range_interval;	// Time between ranging rounds
+	uint8_t MAC[2];			// MAC address of UWB device
+	UWB_range_meas_t measurements; //Raw anchor_distance distances in CM 2*9
+	uint8_t stop; 		// Should be 0x1B
+} __attribute__((packed)) distance_msg_t;
+
+void AppSendRangingDataPX4(phRangingData_t *pRangingData);

+/* semaphore definition */
+#if (APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE == APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_FREERTOS)
+
+/* mutex semaphore */
+#define APP_CONSOLE_CREATE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(mutex) ((mutex) = xSemaphoreCreateMutex())
+
+/* clang-format off */
+#define APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(mutex) \
+{                                                 \
+        if (IS_RUNNING_IN_ISR() == 0U)            \
+        {                                         \
+            (void)xSemaphoreGive(mutex);                \
+        }                                         \
+}
+
+#define APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE_BLOCKING(mutex) \
+{                                                          \
+        if (IS_RUNNING_IN_ISR() == 0U)                     \
+        {                                                  \
+            (void)xSemaphoreTake(mutex, portMAX_DELAY);          \
+        }                                                  \
+}
+
+#define APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE_NONBLOCKING(mutex, result) \
+{                                                                     \
+        if (IS_RUNNING_IN_ISR() == 0U)                                \
+        {                                                             \
+            result = xSemaphoreTake(mutex, 0U);                       \
+        }                                                             \
+        else                                                          \
+        {                                                             \
+            result = 1U;                                              \
+        }                                                             \
+}
+/* clang-format on */
+
+/* Binary semaphore */
+#define APP_CONSOLE_CREATE_BINARY_SEMAPHORE(binary) ((binary) = xSemaphoreCreateBinary())
+#define APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_BINARY_SEMAPHORE_BLOCKING(binary) ((void)xSemaphoreTake(binary, portMAX_DELAY))
+#define APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_BINARY_SEMAPHORE_FROM_ISR(binary) ((void)xSemaphoreGiveFromISR(binary, NULL))

+/*******************************************************************************
+ * Code
+ ******************************************************************************/

+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+
+static void AppConsole_SerialManagerTxCallback(void *callbackParam,
+                                               serial_manager_callback_message_t *message,
+                                               serial_manager_status_t status)
+{
+    app_console_state_struct_t *ioState;
+    uint32_t sendDataLength;
+
+    if ((NULL == callbackParam) || (NULL == message))
+    {
+        return;
+    }
+
+    ioState = (app_console_state_struct_t *)callbackParam;
+
+    ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail += message->length;
+    if (ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail >= ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize)
+    {
+        ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail = 0U;
+    }
+
+    if (kStatus_SerialManager_Success == status)
+    {
+        if (ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail != ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringHead)
+        {
+            if (ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringHead > ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail)
+            {
+                sendDataLength = ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringHead - ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail;
+            }
+            else
+            {
+                sendDataLength = ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize - ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail;
+            }
+
+            (void)SerialManager_WriteNonBlocking(
+                ((serial_write_handle_t)&ioState->serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]),
+                &ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringBuffer[ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail], sendDataLength);
+        }
+    }
+    else if (kStatus_SerialManager_Canceled == status)
+    {
+        ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringTail = 0U;
+        ioState->writeRingBuffer.ringHead = 0U;
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        /*MISRA rule 16.4*/
+    }
+}
+
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE > 0U))
+
+static void AppConsole_SerialManagerRxCallback(void *callbackParam,
+                                               serial_manager_callback_message_t *message,
+                                               serial_manager_status_t status)
+{
+    if ((NULL == callbackParam) || (NULL == message))
+    {
+        return;
+    }
+
+    if (kStatus_SerialManager_Notify == status)
+    {
+    }
+    else if (kStatus_SerialManager_Success == status)
+    {
+        /* release s_appConsoleReadWaitSemaphore from RX callback */
+        APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_BINARY_SEMAPHORE_FROM_ISR(s_appConsoleReadWaitSemaphore);
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        /*MISRA rule 16.4*/
+    }
+}
+#endif
+
+#endif
+
+status_t AppConsole_ReadOneCharacter(uint8_t *ch)
+{
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE > 0U))
+
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING) && \
+    (APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE == APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_BM) && defined(OSA_USED)
+    return kStatus_Fail;
+#else
+    status_t status = (status_t)kStatus_SerialManager_Error;
+
+/* receive one char every time */
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+    status = (status_t)SerialManager_ReadNonBlocking(
+        ((serial_read_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialReadHandleBuffer[0]), ch, 1);
+#else
+    status = (status_t)SerialManager_ReadBlocking(
+        ((serial_read_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialReadHandleBuffer[0]), ch, 1);
+#endif
+    if ((status_t)kStatus_SerialManager_Success != status)
+    {
+        return (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+    }
+    /* wait s_appConsoleReadWaitSemaphore from RX callback */
+    APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_BINARY_SEMAPHORE_BLOCKING(s_appConsoleReadWaitSemaphore);
+
+    return (status_t)kStatus_Success;
+#endif
+
+#else
+
+    return (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+
+#endif
+}
+
+#if APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO_FUNCTION
+static status_t AppConsole_EchoCharacter(uint8_t *ch, bool isGetChar, int *index)
+{
+    /* Due to scanf take \n and \r as end of string,should not echo */
+    if (((*ch != (uint8_t)'\r') && (*ch != (uint8_t)'\n')) || (isGetChar))
+    {
+        /* receive one char every time */
+        if (1 != AppConsole_SendDataReliable(ch, 1U))
+        {
+            return (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+        }
+    }
+
+    if ((!isGetChar) && (index != NULL))
+    {
+        if (APP_CONSOLE_BACKSPACE == *ch)
+        {
+            if ((*index >= 2))
+            {
+                *index -= 2;
+            }
+            else
+            {
+                *index = 0;
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    return (status_t)kStatus_Success;
+}
+#endif
+
+int AppConsole_SendData(uint8_t *ch, size_t size)
+{
+    status_t status = (status_t)kStatus_SerialManager_Error;
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+    uint32_t sendDataLength;
+    int txBusy = 0;
+#endif
+    assert(NULL != ch);
+    assert(0 != size);
+
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+    uint32_t regPrimask = DisableGlobalIRQ();
+    if (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead != s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail)
+    {
+        txBusy = 1;
+        sendDataLength =
+            (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead + s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize -
+             s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail) %
+            s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize;
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        sendDataLength = 0U;
+    }
+    sendDataLength = s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize - sendDataLength - 1;
+    if (sendDataLength <= size)
+    {
+        EnableGlobalIRQ(regPrimask);
+        return -1;
+    }
+    for (int i = 0; i < (int)size; i++)
+    {
+        s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBuffer[s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead++] = ch[i];
+        if (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead >= s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize)
+        {
+            s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead = 0U;
+        }
+    }
+
+    status = (status_t)kStatus_SerialManager_Success;
+
+    if (txBusy == 0)
+    {
+        if (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead > s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail)
+        {
+            sendDataLength =
+                s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead - s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail;
+        }
+        else
+        {
+            sendDataLength =
+                s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize - s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail;
+        }
+
+        status = (status_t)SerialManager_WriteNonBlocking(
+            ((serial_write_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]),
+            &s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBuffer[s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail],
+            sendDataLength);
+    }
+    EnableGlobalIRQ(regPrimask);
+#else
+    status = (status_t)SerialManager_WriteBlocking(
+        ((serial_write_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]), ch, size);
+#endif
+    return (((status_t)kStatus_Success == status) ? (int)size : -1);
+}
+
+int AppConsole_SendDataReliable(uint8_t *ch, size_t size)
+{
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE > 0U))
+    status_t status = kStatus_SerialManager_Error;
+    uint32_t sendDataLength;
+    uint32_t totalLength = size;
+    int sentLength;
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE */
+#else
+    status_t status = kStatus_SerialManager_Error;
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING */
+
+    assert(NULL != ch);
+    assert(0 != size);
+
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE > 0U))
+    do
+    {
+        uint32_t regPrimask = DisableGlobalIRQ();
+        if (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead != s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail)
+        {
+            sendDataLength =
+                (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead + s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize -
+                 s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail) %
+                s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize;
+        }
+        else
+        {
+            sendDataLength = 0U;
+        }
+        sendDataLength = s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize - sendDataLength - 1U;
+
+        if (sendDataLength > 0U)
+        {
+            if (sendDataLength > totalLength)
+            {
+                sendDataLength = totalLength;
+            }
+
+            sentLength = AppConsole_SendData(&ch[size - totalLength], sendDataLength);
+            if (sentLength > 0)
+            {
+                totalLength = totalLength - (uint32_t)sentLength;
+            }
+        }
+        EnableGlobalIRQ(regPrimask);
+
+        if (totalLength != 0U)
+        {
+            status = AppConsole_Flush();
+            if ((status_t)kStatus_Success != status)
+            {
+                break;
+            }
+        }
+    } while (totalLength != 0U);
+    return (status_t)(uint32_t)((uint32_t)size - totalLength);
+#else
+    return AppConsole_SendData(ch, size);
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE */
+
+#else
+    status          = (status_t)SerialManager_WriteBlocking(
+        ((serial_write_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]), ch, size);
+    return (((status_t)kStatus_Success == status) ? (int)size : -1);
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING */
+}
+
+int AppConsole_ReadLine(uint8_t *buf, size_t size)
+{
+    int i = 0;
+
+    assert(buf != NULL);
+
+    /* take mutex lock function */
+    APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE_BLOCKING(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+
+    do
+    {
+        /* recieve one char every time */
+        if ((status_t)kStatus_Success != AppConsole_ReadOneCharacter(&buf[i]))
+        {
+            /* release mutex lock function */
+            APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+            i = -1;
+            break;
+        }
+#if APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO_FUNCTION
+        (void)AppConsole_EchoCharacter(&buf[i], false, &i);
+#endif
+        /* analysis data */
+        if (((uint8_t)'\r' == buf[i]) || ((uint8_t)'\n' == buf[i]))
+        {
+            /* End of Line. */
+            if (0 == i)
+            {
+                buf[i] = (uint8_t)'\0';
+                continue;
+            }
+            else
+            {
+                break;
+            }
+        }
+        i++;
+    } while (i < (int)size);
+
+    /* get char should not add '\0'*/
+    if (i == (int)size)
+    {
+        buf[i] = (uint8_t)'\0';
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        buf[i + 1] = (uint8_t)'\0';
+    }
+
+    /* release mutex lock function */
+    APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+
+    return i;
+}
+
+int AppConsole_ReadCharacter(uint8_t *ch)
+{
+    int ret;
+
+    assert(ch);
+
+    /* take mutex lock function */
+    APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE_BLOCKING(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+    /* read one character */
+    if ((status_t)kStatus_Success == AppConsole_ReadOneCharacter(ch))
+    {
+        ret = 1;
+#if APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO_FUNCTION
+        (void)AppConsole_EchoCharacter(ch, true, NULL);
+#endif
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        ret = -1;
+    }
+
+    /* release mutex lock function */
+    APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+
+    return ret;
+}
+
+#if SDK_APPCONSOLE
+static void AppConsole_PrintCallback(char *buf, int32_t *indicator, char appVal, int len)
+{
+    int i = 0;
+
+    for (i = 0; i < len; i++)
+    {
+        if (((uint32_t)*indicator + 1UL) >= APP_CONSOLE_PRINTF_MAX_LOG_LEN)
+        {
+            (void)AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)buf, (uint32_t)(*indicator));
+            *indicator = 0;
+        }
+
+        buf[*indicator] = appVal;
+        (*indicator)++;
+    }
+}
+#endif
+
+/*************Code for AppConsole Init, Deinit, Printf, Scanf *******************************/
+
+/* See fsl_app_console.h for documentation of this function. */
+status_t AppConsole_Init(uint8_t instance, uint32_t baudRate, serial_port_type_t device, uint32_t clkSrcFreq)
+{
+    serial_manager_config_t serialConfig;
+    status_t status = (status_t)kStatus_SerialManager_Error;
+
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_UART) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_UART > 0U))
+    serial_port_uart_config_t uartConfig = {
+        .instance     = instance,
+        .clockRate    = clkSrcFreq,
+        .baudRate     = baudRate,
+        .parityMode   = kSerialManager_UartParityDisabled,
+        .stopBitCount = kSerialManager_UartOneStopBit,
+        .enableRx     = 1,
+        .enableTx     = 1,
+    };
+#endif
+
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC > 0U))
+    serial_port_usb_cdc_config_t usbCdcConfig = {
+        .controllerIndex = (serial_port_usb_cdc_controller_index_t)instance,
+    };
+#endif
+
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_SWO) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_SWO > 0U))
+    serial_port_swo_config_t swoConfig = {
+        .clockRate = clkSrcFreq,
+        .baudRate  = baudRate,
+        .port      = instance,
+        .protocol  = kSerialManager_SwoProtocolNrz,
+    };
+#endif
+
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC_VIRTUAL) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC_VIRTUAL > 0U))
+    serial_port_usb_cdc_virtual_config_t usbCdcVirtualConfig = {
+        .controllerIndex = (serial_port_usb_cdc_virtual_controller_index_t)instance,
+    };
+#endif
+    serialConfig.type = device;
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+    serialConfig.ringBuffer     = &s_appConsoleState.readRingBuffer[0];
+    serialConfig.ringBufferSize = APP_CONSOLE_RECEIVE_BUFFER_LEN;
+#endif
+
+    if (kSerialPort_Uart == device)
+    {
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_UART) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_UART > 0U))
+        serialConfig.portConfig = &uartConfig;
+#else
+        return status;
+#endif
+    }
+    else if (kSerialPort_UsbCdc == device)
+    {
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC > 0U))
+        serialConfig.portConfig = &usbCdcConfig;
+#else
+        return status;
+#endif
+    }
+    else if (kSerialPort_Swo == device)
+    {
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_SWO) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_SWO > 0U))
+        serialConfig.portConfig = &swoConfig;
+#else
+        return status;
+#endif
+    }
+    else if (kSerialPort_UsbCdcVirtual == device)
+    {
+#if (defined(SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC_VIRTUAL) && (SERIAL_PORT_TYPE_USBCDC_VIRTUAL > 0U))
+        serialConfig.portConfig = &usbCdcVirtualConfig;
+#else
+        return status;
+#endif
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        return status;
+    }
+
+    (void)memset(&s_appConsoleState, 0, sizeof(s_appConsoleState));
+
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+    s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringBufferSize = APP_CONSOLE_TRANSMIT_BUFFER_LEN;
+#endif
+
+    s_appConsoleState.serialHandle = (serial_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialHandleBuffer[0];
+    status                           = (status_t)SerialManager_Init(s_appConsoleState.serialHandle, &serialConfig);
+
+    assert(kStatus_SerialManager_Success == status);
+
+    APP_CONSOLE_CREATE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE > 0U))
+    APP_CONSOLE_CREATE_BINARY_SEMAPHORE(s_appConsoleReadWaitSemaphore);
+#endif
+
+    {
+        status = (status_t)SerialManager_OpenWriteHandle(
+            s_appConsoleState.serialHandle, ((serial_write_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]));
+        assert(kStatus_SerialManager_Success == status);
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+        (void)SerialManager_InstallTxCallback(((serial_write_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]),
+                                              AppConsole_SerialManagerTxCallback, &s_appConsoleState);
+#endif
+    }
+
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE > 0U))
+    {
+        status = (status_t)SerialManager_OpenReadHandle(
+            s_appConsoleState.serialHandle, ((serial_read_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialReadHandleBuffer[0]));
+        assert(kStatus_SerialManager_Success == status);
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+        (void)SerialManager_InstallRxCallback(((serial_read_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialReadHandleBuffer[0]),
+                                              AppConsole_SerialManagerRxCallback, &s_appConsoleState);
+#endif
+    }
+#endif
+
+    g_serialHandleApp = s_appConsoleState.serialHandle;
+
+    return kStatus_Success;
+}
+
+/* See fsl_app_console.h for documentation of this function. */
+status_t AppConsole_Deinit(void)
+{
+    {
+        if (s_appConsoleState.serialHandle != NULL)
+        {
+            (void)SerialManager_CloseWriteHandle(
+                ((serial_write_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialWriteHandleBuffer[0]));
+        }
+    }
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE > 0U))
+    {
+        if (s_appConsoleState.serialHandle != NULL)
+        {
+            (void)SerialManager_CloseReadHandle(((serial_read_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialReadHandleBuffer[0]));
+        }
+    }
+#endif
+    if (s_appConsoleState.serialHandle)
+    {
+        if (kStatus_SerialManager_Success == SerialManager_Deinit(s_appConsoleState.serialHandle))
+        {
+            s_appConsoleState.serialHandle = NULL;
+            g_serialHandleApp                   = NULL;
+        }
+    }
+    return (status_t)kStatus_Success;
+}
+
+#if ((SDK_APPCONSOLE > 0U) ||                                                   \
+     ((SDK_APPCONSOLE == 0U) && defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING) && \
+      (defined(APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE > 0U))))
+APP_CONSOLE_FUNCTION_PREFIX status_t AppConsole_Flush(void)
+{
+#if defined(APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING)
+
+#if (APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE == APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_BM) && defined(OSA_USED)
+
+    if (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead != s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail)
+    {
+        return (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+    }
+
+#else
+
+    while (s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringHead != s_appConsoleState.writeRingBuffer.ringTail)
+    {
+#if (APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE == APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_FREERTOS)
+        if (0U == IS_RUNNING_IN_ISR())
+        {
+            if (taskSCHEDULER_RUNNING == xTaskGetSchedulerState())
+            {
+                vTaskDelay(1);
+            }
+        }
+        else
+        {
+            return (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+        }
+#endif
+    }
+
+#endif
+
+#endif
+    return (status_t)kStatus_Success;
+}
+#endif
+
+#if SDK_APPCONSOLE
+/* See fsl_app_console.h for documentation of this function. */
+int AppConsole_Printf(const char *formatString, ...)
+{
+    va_list ap;
+    int logLength = 0, appResult = 0;
+    char printBuf[APP_CONSOLE_PRINTF_MAX_LOG_LEN] = {'\0'};
+
+    if (NULL == g_serialHandleApp)
+    {
+        return 0;
+    }
+
+    va_start(ap, formatString);
+    /* format print log first */
+    logLength = StrFormatPrintf(formatString, ap, printBuf, AppConsole_PrintCallback);
+    /* print log */
+    appResult = AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)printBuf, (size_t)logLength);
+
+    va_end(ap);
+
+    return appResult;
+}
+
+/* See fsl_app_console.h for documentation of this function. */
+int AppConsole_Putchar(int ch)
+{
+    /* print char */
+    return AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)&ch, 1U);
+}
+
+/* See fsl_app_console.h for documentation of this function. */
+int AppConsole_Scanf(char *formatString, ...)
+{
+    va_list ap;
+    int formatResult;
+    char scanfBuf[APP_CONSOLE_SCANF_MAX_LOG_LEN + 1U] = {'\0'};
+
+    /* scanf log */
+    (void)AppConsole_ReadLine((uint8_t *)scanfBuf, APP_CONSOLE_SCANF_MAX_LOG_LEN);
+    /* get va_list */
+    va_start(ap, formatString);
+    /* format scanf log */
+    formatResult = StrFormatScanf(scanfBuf, formatString, ap);
+
+    va_end(ap);
+
+    return formatResult;
+}
+
+#ifdef APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING
+status_t AppConsole_TryGetchar(char *ch)
+{
+#if (defined(APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE) && (APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE > 0U))
+    uint32_t length = 0;
+    status_t status = (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+
+    assert(ch);
+
+    /* take mutex lock function */
+    APP_CONSOLE_TAKE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE_BLOCKING(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+
+    if (kStatus_SerialManager_Success ==
+        SerialManager_TryRead(((serial_read_handle_t)&s_appConsoleState.serialReadHandleBuffer[0]), (uint8_t *)ch, 1,
+                              &length))
+    {
+        if (length != 0U)
+        {
+#if APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO_FUNCTION
+            (void)AppConsole_EchoCharacter((uint8_t *)ch, true, NULL);
+#endif
+            status = (status_t)kStatus_Success;
+        }
+    }
+    /* release mutex lock function */
+    APP_CONSOLE_GIVE_MUTEX_SEMAPHORE(s_appConsoleReadSemaphore);
+    return status;
+#else
+    return (status_t)kStatus_Fail;
+#endif
+}
+#endif
+
+/* See fsl_app_console.h for documentation of this function. */
+int AppConsole_Getchar(void)
+{
+    uint8_t ch = 0U;
+
+    /* Get char */
+    (void)AppConsole_ReadCharacter(&ch);
+
+    return (int)ch;
+}
+
+#endif /* SDK_APPCONSOLE */
+
+/*************Code to support toolchain's printf, scanf *******************************/
+/* These function __write and __read is used to support IAR tool-chain to printf and scanf*/
+#if (defined(__ICCARM__))
+#if defined(SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART)
+#pragma weak __write
+size_t __write(int handle, const unsigned char *buffer, size_t size)
+{
+    if (buffer == 0)
+    {
+        /*
+         * This means that we should flush internal buffers.  Since we don't we just return.
+         * (Remember, "handle" == -1 means that all handles should be flushed.)
+         */
+        return 0;
+    }
+
+    /* This function only writes to "standard out" and "standard err" for all other file handles it returns failure. */
+    if ((handle != 1) && (handle != 2))
+    {
+        return ((size_t)-1);
+    }
+
+    /* Send data. */
+    AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)buffer, size);
+
+    return size;
+}
+
+#pragma weak __read
+size_t __read(int handle, unsigned char *buffer, size_t size)
+{
+    uint8_t ch     = 0U;
+    int actualSize = 0U;
+
+    /* This function only reads from "standard in", for all other file  handles it returns failure. */
+    if (handle != 0)
+    {
+        return ((size_t)-1);
+    }
+
+    /* Receive data.*/
+    for (; size > 0; size--)
+    {
+        AppConsole_ReadCharacter(&ch);
+        if (ch == 0)
+        {
+            break;
+        }
+
+        *buffer++ = ch;
+        actualSize++;
+    }
+
+    return actualSize;
+}
+#endif /* SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART */
+
+/* support LPC Xpresso with RedLib */
+#elif (defined(__REDLIB__))
+
+#if (defined(SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART))
+int __attribute__((weak)) __sys_write(int handle, char *buffer, int size)
+{
+    if (buffer == 0)
+    {
+        /* return -1 if error. */
+        return -1;
+    }
+
+    /* This function only writes to "standard out" and "standard err" for all other file handles it returns failure. */
+    if ((handle != 1) && (handle != 2))
+    {
+        return -1;
+    }
+
+    /* Send data. */
+    AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)buffer, size);
+
+    return 0;
+}
+
+int __attribute__((weak)) __sys_readc(void)
+{
+    char tmp;
+
+    /* Receive data. */
+    AppConsole_ReadCharacter((uint8_t *)&tmp);
+
+    return tmp;
+}
+#endif
+
+/* These function fputc and fgetc is used to support KEIL tool-chain to printf and scanf*/
+#elif defined(__CC_ARM) || defined(__ARMCC_VERSION)
+#if defined(SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART)
+#if defined(__CC_ARM)
+struct __FILE
+{
+    int handle;
+    /*
+     * Whatever you require here. If the only file you are using is standard output using printf() for appging,
+     * no file handling is required.
+     */
+};
+#endif
+
+/* FILE is typedef in stdio.h. */
+#pragma weak __stdout
+#pragma weak __stdin
+FILE __stdout;
+FILE __stdin;
+
+#pragma weak fputc
+int fputc(int ch, FILE *f)
+{
+    /* Send data. */
+    return AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)(&ch), 1);
+}
+
+#pragma weak fgetc
+int fgetc(FILE *f)
+{
+    char ch;
+
+    /* Receive data. */
+    AppConsole_ReadCharacter((uint8_t *)&ch);
+
+    return ch;
+}
+
+/*
+ * Terminate the program, passing a return code back to the user.
+ * This function may not return.
+ */
+void _sys_exit(int returncode)
+{
+    while (1)
+    {
+    }
+}
+
+/*
+ * Writes a character to the output channel. This function is used
+ * for last-resort error message output.
+ */
+void _ttywrch(int ch)
+{
+    char ench = ch;
+    AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)(&ench), 1);
+}
+
+char *_sys_command_string(char *cmd, int len)
+{
+    return (cmd);
+}
+#endif /* SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART */
+
+/* These function __write and __read is used to support ARM_GCC, KDS, Atollic toolchains to printf and scanf*/
+#elif (defined(__GNUC__))
+
+#if ((defined(__GNUC__) && (!defined(__MCUXPRESSO)) && (defined(SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART))) || \
+     (defined(__MCUXPRESSO) && (defined(SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART))))
+int __attribute__((weak)) _write(int handle, char *buffer, int size);
+int __attribute__((weak)) _write(int handle, char *buffer, int size)
+{
+    if (buffer == NULL)
+    {
+        /* return -1 if error. */
+        return -1;
+    }
+
+    /* This function only writes to "standard out" and "standard err" for all other file handles it returns failure. */
+    if ((handle != 1) && (handle != 2))
+    {
+        return -1;
+    }
+
+    /* Send data. */
+    (void)AppConsole_SendDataReliable((uint8_t *)buffer, (size_t)size);
+
+    return size;
+}
+
+int __attribute__((weak)) _read(int handle, char *buffer, int size);
+int __attribute__((weak)) _read(int handle, char *buffer, int size)
+{
+    uint8_t ch     = 0U;
+    int actualSize = 0;
+
+    /* This function only reads from "standard in", for all other file handles it returns failure. */
+    if (handle != 0)
+    {
+        return -1;
+    }
+
+    /* Receive data. */
+    for (; size > 0; size--)
+    {
+        if (AppConsole_ReadCharacter(&ch) < 0)
+        {
+            break;
+        }
+
+        *buffer++ = (char)ch;
+        actualSize++;
+
+        if ((ch == 0U) || (ch == (uint8_t)'\n') || (ch == (uint8_t)'\r'))
+        {
+            break;
+        }
+    }
+
+    return (actualSize > 0) ? actualSize : -1;
+}
+#endif
+
+#endif /* __ICCARM__ */

+/*
+ * Copyright (c) 2013 - 2015, Freescale Semiconductor, Inc.
+ * Copyright 2016-2018 NXP
+ * Copyright 2022-2023 NXP
+ * All rights reserved.
+ *
+ * SPDX-License-Identifier: BSD-3-Clause
+ *
+ * App console shall provide input and output functions to scan and print formatted data.
+ * o Support a format specifier for PRINTF follows this prototype "%[flags][width][.precision][length]specifier"
+ *   - [flags] :'-', '+', '#', ' ', '0'
+ *   - [width]:  number (0,1...)
+ *   - [.precision]: number (0,1...)
+ *   - [length]: do not support
+ *   - [specifier]: 'd', 'i', 'f', 'F', 'x', 'X', 'o', 'p', 'u', 'c', 's', 'n'
+ * o Support a format specifier for SCANF follows this prototype " %[*][width][length]specifier"
+ *   - [*]: is supported.
+ *   - [width]: number (0,1...)
+ *   - [length]: 'h', 'hh', 'l','ll','L'. ignore ('j','z','t')
+ *   - [specifier]: 'd', 'i', 'u', 'f', 'F', 'e', 'E', 'g', 'G', 'a', 'A', 'o', 'c', 's'
+ */
+
+#ifndef _FSL_APPCONSOLE_H_
+#define _FSL_APPCONSOLE_H_
+
+#include "fsl_common.h"
+#include "serial_manager.h"
+
+/*!
+ * @addtogroup appconsole
+ * @{
+ */
+
+/*******************************************************************************
+ * Definitions
+ ******************************************************************************/
+
+extern serial_handle_t g_serialHandleApp; /*!< serial manager handle */
+
+/*! @brief Definition select redirect tool-chain printf, scanf to uart or not. */
+#define APPCONSOLE_REDIRECT_TO_TOOLCHAIN 0U /*!< Select tool-chain printf and scanf. */
+#define APPCONSOLE_REDIRECT_TO_SDK 1U       /*!< Select SDK version printf, scanf. */
+#define APPCONSOLE_DISABLE 2U               /*!< Disable appconsole function. */
+
+/*! @brief Definition to select sdk or tool-chain printf, scanf. The macro only support
+ * to be redefined in project setting.
+ */
+#ifndef SDK_APPCONSOLE
+#define SDK_APPCONSOLE 1U
+#endif
+
+/*! @brief whether provide low level IO implementation to tool-chain printf and scanf.
+ * For example, within MCUXpresso, if the macro SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART is defined,
+ * __sys_write and __sys_readc will be used when __REDLIB__ is defined;
+ * _write and _read will be used in other cases.
+ * If the macro SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART is not defined, the semihost will be used.
+ */
+#ifndef SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART
+/* mcux will handle this macro, not define it here */
+#if (!defined(__MCUXPRESSO))
+#define SDK_APPCONSOLE_UART
+#endif
+#endif
+
+#if defined(SDK_APPCONSOLE) && !(SDK_APPCONSOLE)
+#include <stdio.h>
+#endif
+
+/*! @brief Definition to select redirect tool-chain printf, scanf to uart or not.
+ *
+ *  if SDK_APPCONSOLE defined to 0,it represents select tool-chain printf, scanf.
+ *  if SDK_APPCONSOLE defined to 1,it represents select SDK version printf, scanf.
+ *  if SDK_APPCONSOLE defined to 2,it represents disable appconsole function.
+ */
+#if SDK_APPCONSOLE == APPCONSOLE_DISABLE /* Disable app console */
+#define PRINTF(...) \
+    do              \
+    {               \
+    } while (0)
+#define SCANF(...) \
+    do             \
+    {              \
+    } while (0)
+#define PUTCHAR(...) \
+    do               \
+    {                \
+    } while (0)
+#define GETCHAR() -1
+#elif SDK_APPCONSOLE == APPCONSOLE_REDIRECT_TO_SDK /* Select printf, scanf, putchar, getchar of SDK version. */
+#define APPPRINTF AppConsole_Printf
+#define APPSCANF AppConsole_Scanf
+#define APPPUTCHAR AppConsole_Putchar
+#define APPGETCHAR AppConsole_Getchar
+#define APPSENDDATA AppConsole_SendData
+#elif SDK_APPCONSOLE == APPCONSOLE_REDIRECT_TO_TOOLCHAIN /* Select printf, scanf, putchar, getchar of tool-chain. \ \
+                                                              */
+#define PRINTF printf
+#define SCANF scanf
+#define PUTCHAR putchar
+#define GETCHAR getchar
+#endif /* SDK_APPCONSOLE */
+
+/*******************************************************************************
+ * Prototypes
+ ******************************************************************************/
+
+#if defined(__cplusplus)
+extern "C" {
+#endif /* __cplusplus */
+
+/*! @name Initialization*/
+/* @{ */
+
+/*!
+ * @brief Initializes the peripheral used for app messages.
+ *
+ * Call this function to enable app log messages to be output via the specified peripheral
+ * initialized by the serial manager module.
+ * After this function has returned, stdout and stdin are connected to the selected peripheral.
+ *
+ * @param instance      The instance of the module.
+ * @param baudRate      The desired baud rate in bits per second.
+ * @param device        Low level device type for the app console, can be one of the following.
+ *                      @arg kSerialPort_Uart,
+ *                      @arg kSerialPort_UsbCdc
+ *                      @arg kSerialPort_UsbCdcVirtual.
+ * @param clkSrcFreq    Frequency of peripheral source clock.
+ *
+ * @return              Indicates whether initialization was successful or not.
+ * @retval kStatus_Success          Execution successfully
+ */
+status_t AppConsole_Init(uint8_t instance, uint32_t baudRate, serial_port_type_t device, uint32_t clkSrcFreq);
+
+/*!
+ * @brief De-initializes the peripheral used for app messages.
+ *
+ * Call this function to disable   log messages to be output via the specified peripheral
+ * initialized by the serial manager module.
+ *
+ * @return Indicates whether de-initialization was successful or not.
+ */
+status_t AppConsole_Deinit(void);
+
+#if SDK_APPCONSOLE
+/*!
+ * @brief Writes formatted output to the standard output stream.
+ *
+ * Call this function to write a formatted output to the standard output stream.
+ *
+ * @param   formatString Format control string.
+ * @return  Returns the number of characters printed or a negative value if an error occurs.
+ */
+int AppConsole_Printf(const char *formatString, ...);
+
+/*!
+ * @brief Writes a character to stdout.
+ *
+ * Call this function to write a character to stdout.
+ *
+ * @param   ch Character to be written.
+ * @return  Returns the character written.
+ */
+int AppConsole_Putchar(int ch);
+
+/*!
+ * @brief Reads formatted data from the standard input stream.
+ *
+ * Call this function to read formatted data from the standard input stream.
+ *
+ * @note Due the limitation in the BM OSA environment (CPU is blocked in the function,
+ * other tasks will not be scheduled), the function cannot be used when the
+ * APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING is set in the BM OSA environment.
+ * And an error is returned when the function called in this case. The suggestion
+ * is that polling the non-blocking function AppConsole_TryGetchar to get the input char.
+ *
+ * @param   formatString Format control string.
+ * @return  Returns the number of fields successfully converted and assigned.
+ */
+int AppConsole_Scanf(char *formatString, ...);
+
+/*!
+ * @brief Reads a character from standard input.
+ *
+ * Call this function to read a character from standard input.
+ *
+ * @note Due the limitation in the BM OSA environment (CPU is blocked in the function,
+ * other tasks will not be scheduled), the function cannot be used when the
+ * APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING is set in the BM OSA environment.
+ * And an error is returned when the function called in this case. The suggestion
+ * is that polling the non-blocking function AppConsole_TryGetchar to get the input char.
+ *
+ * @return Returns the character read.
+ */
+int AppConsole_Getchar(void);
+
+/*!
+ * @brief App console flush.
+ *
+ * Call this function to wait the tx buffer empty.
+ * If interrupt transfer is using, make sure the global IRQ is enable before call this function
+ * This function should be called when
+ * 1, before enter power down mode
+ * 2, log is required to print to terminal immediately
+ * @return Indicates whether wait idle was successful or not.
+ */
+status_t AppConsole_Flush(void);
+
+#ifdef APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING
+/*!
+ * @brief App console try to get char
+ * This function provides a API which will not block current task, if character is
+ * available return it, otherwise return fail.
+ * @param ch the address of char to receive
+ * @return Indicates get char was successful or not.
+ */
+status_t AppConsole_TryGetchar(char *ch);
+#endif
+
+#endif /* SDK_APPCONSOLE */
+
+/*! @} */
+
+#if defined(__cplusplus)
+}
+#endif /* __cplusplus */
+
+/*! @} */
+
+#endif /* _FSL_APPCONSOLE_H_ */

+/*
+ * Copyright 2017 - 2019 NXP
+ * Copyright 2022 - 2023 NXP
+ * All rights reserved.
+ *
+ *
+ * SPDX-License-Identifier: BSD-3-Clause
+ */
+#ifndef _FSL_APP_CONSOLE_CONF_H_
+#define _FSL_APP_CONSOLE_CONF_H_
+
+/****************App console configuration********************/
+
+/*! @brief If Non-blocking mode is needed, please define it at project setting,
+ * otherwise blocking mode is the default transfer mode.
+ * Warning: If you want to use non-blocking transfer,please make sure the corresponding
+ * IO interrupt is enable, otherwise there is no output.
+ * And non-blocking is combine with buffer, no matter bare-metal or rtos.
+ * Below shows how to configure in your project if you want to use non-blocking mode.
+ * For IAR, right click project and select "Options", define it in "C/C++ Compiler->Preprocessor->Defined symbols".
+ * For KEIL, click "Options for Target", define it in "C/C++->Preprocessor Symbols->Define".
+ * For ARMGCC, open CmakeLists.txt and add the following lines,
+ * "SET(CMAKE_C_FLAGS_APP "${CMAKE_C_FLAGS_APP} -DAPP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING")" for debug target.
+ * "SET(CMAKE_C_FLAGS_RELEASE "${CMAKE_C_FLAGS_RELEASE} -DAPP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING")" for release target.
+ * For MCUxpresso, right click project and select "Properties", define it in "C/C++ Build->Settings->MCU C
+ * Complier->Preprocessor".
+ *
+ */
+#ifdef APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING
+/*! @brief define the transmit buffer length which is used to store the multi task log, buffer is enabled automatically
+ * when
+ * non-blocking transfer is using,
+ * This value will affect the RAM's utilization, should be set per paltform's capability and software requirement.
+ * If it is configured too small, log maybe missed , because the log will not be
+ * buffered if the buffer is full, and the print will return immediately with -1.
+ * And this value should be multiple of 4 to meet memory alignment.
+ *
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_TRANSMIT_BUFFER_LEN
+#define APP_CONSOLE_TRANSMIT_BUFFER_LEN (512U)
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TRANSMIT_BUFFER_LEN */
+
+/*! @brief define the receive buffer length which is used to store the user input, buffer is enabled automatically when
+ * non-blocking transfer is using,
+ * This value will affect the RAM's utilization, should be set per paltform's capability and software requirement.
+ * If it is configured too small, log maybe missed, because buffer will be overwritten if buffer is too small.
+ * And this value should be a multiple of 4 to meet memory alignment.
+ *
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_RECEIVE_BUFFER_LEN
+#define APP_CONSOLE_RECEIVE_BUFFER_LEN (1024U)
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_RECEIVE_BUFFER_LEN */
+
+/*!@ brief Whether enable the reliable TX function
+ * If the macro is zero, the reliable TX function of the debug console is disabled.
+ * When the macro is zero, the string of PRINTF will be thrown away after the transmit buffer is full.
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE
+#define APP_CONSOLE_TX_RELIABLE_ENABLE (1U)
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE */
+
+#else
+#define APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_BLOCKING
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING */
+
+/*!@ brief Whether enable the RX function
+ * If the macro is zero, the receive function of the debug console is disabled.
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE
+#define APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE (1U)
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_RX_ENABLE */
+
+/*!@ brief define the MAX log length debug console support , that is when you call printf("log", x);, the log
+ * length can not bigger than this value.
+ * This macro decide the local log buffer length, the buffer locate at stack, the stack maybe overflow if
+ * the buffer is too big and current task stack size not big enough.
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_PRINTF_MAX_LOG_LEN
+#define APP_CONSOLE_PRINTF_MAX_LOG_LEN (128U)
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_PRINTF_MAX_LOG_LEN */
+
+/*!@ brief define the buffer support buffer scanf log length, that is when you call scanf("log", &x);, the log
+ * length can not bigger than this value.
+ * As same as the APP_CONSOLE_BUFFER_PRINTF_MAX_LOG_LEN.
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_SCANF_MAX_LOG_LEN
+#define APP_CONSOLE_SCANF_MAX_LOG_LEN (20U)
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_SCANF_MAX_LOG_LEN */
+
+/*! @brief App console synchronization
+ * User should not change these macro for synchronization mode, but add the
+ * corresponding synchronization mechanism per different software environment.
+ * Such as, if another RTOS is used,
+ * add:
+ *  #define APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_XXXX 3
+ * in this configuration file and implement the synchronization in fsl.log.c.
+ */
+/*! @brief synchronization for baremetal software */
+#define APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_BM 0
+/*! @brief synchronization for freertos software */
+#define APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_FREERTOS 1
+
+/*! @brief RTOS synchronization mechanism disable
+ * If not defined, default is enabled, to avoid multitask log print mess.
+ * If other RTOS is used, you can implement the RTOS's specific synchronization mechanism in fsl.log.c
+ * If synchronization is disabled, log maybe messed on terminal.
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_DISABLE_RTOS_SYNCHRONIZATION
+#ifdef APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING
+#ifdef FSL_RTOS_FREE_RTOS
+#define APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_FREERTOS
+#else
+#define APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_BM
+#endif /* FSL_RTOS_FREE_RTOS */
+#else
+#define APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_MODE APP_CONSOLE_SYNCHRONIZATION_BM
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_TRANSFER_NON_BLOCKING */
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_DISABLE_RTOS_SYNCHRONIZATION */
+
+/*! @brief echo function support
+ * If you want to use the echo function,please define APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO
+ * at your project setting.
+ */
+#ifndef APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO
+#define APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO_FUNCTION 0
+#else
+#define APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO_FUNCTION 1
+#endif /* APP_CONSOLE_ENABLE_ECHO */
+
+/*********************************************************************/
+
+/***************App console other configuration*********************/
+/*! @brief Definition to printf the float number. */
+#ifndef PRINTF_FLOAT_ENABLE
+#define PRINTF_FLOAT_ENABLE 0U
+#endif /* PRINTF_FLOAT_ENABLE */
+
+/*! @brief Definition to scanf the float number. */
+#ifndef SCANF_FLOAT_ENABLE
+#define SCANF_FLOAT_ENABLE 0U
+#endif /* SCANF_FLOAT_ENABLE */
+
+/*! @brief Definition to support advanced format specifier for printf. */
+#ifndef PRINTF_ADVANCED_ENABLE
+#define PRINTF_ADVANCED_ENABLE 0U
+#endif /* PRINTF_ADVANCED_ENABLE */
+
+/*! @brief Definition to support advanced format specifier for scanf. */
+#ifndef SCANF_ADVANCED_ENABLE
+#define SCANF_ADVANCED_ENABLE 0U
+#endif /* SCANF_ADVANCED_ENABLE */
+
+/*! @brief Definition to select virtual com(USB CDC) as the debug console. */
+#ifndef BOARD_USE_VIRTUALCOM
+#define BOARD_USE_VIRTUALCOM 0U
+#endif
+/*******************************************************************/
+
+#endif /* _FSL_APP_CONSOLE_CONF_H_ */
